json.data.result?.imageUrl,\n    error: json.data.error,\n  };\n}\n\n/** 完整异步工作流：提交 → 轮询 → 返回图片 URL */\nasync function generateImage(prompt: string): Promise<string> {\n  const taskId = await submitImageGeneration(prompt);\n\n  const POLL_INTERVAL_MS = 7000;\n  const TIMEOUT_MS = 10 * 60 * 1000;\n  const deadline = Date.now() + TIMEOUT_MS;\n\n  while (Date.now() < deadline) {\n    await minutes`);\n}\n```\n\n**生成期文件下载（必须执行）：**\n\n生成接口返回的 URL 是 CDN 临时链接，在生成期（Agent 直接调用场景）获得 URL 后，**必须立即使用 Bash 工具将文件下载到本地**，以便用户查看结果。\n\n```bash\ncurl -L -o <本地路径> "<生成的文件 # ─── 辅助函数 ────────────────────────────────────────
```
def submit_task(prompt: str) -> str:
    body = {"contents": [{"parts": [{"text": prompt}]}]}
    r = requests.post(SUBMIT_URL, headers=GEN_HEADERS, json=body, timeout=30)
    r.raise_for_status()
    data = r.json()
    if data.get("status") != 0:
        raise RuntimeError(f"提交失败: {data}")
    return data["data"]["taskId"]

def query_task(task_id: str) -> dict:
    r = requests.post(QUERY_URL, headers=GEN_HEADERS, json={"taskId": task_id}, timeout=30)
    r.raise_for_status()
    data = r.json()
    if data.get("status") != 0:
        raise RuntimeError(f"查询失败: {data}")
    return data["data"]

def wait_for_result(task_id: str, timeout_s=600) -> str:
    deadline = time.time() + timeout_s
    while time.time() < deadline:
        time.sleep(7)
        result = query_task(task_id)
        st = result.get("status")
        if st == "SUCCESS":
            url = result["result"]["imageUrl"]
            print(f"  ✓ {task_id[:16]}… → {url[:60]}…")
            return url
        elif st == "FAILED":
            raise RuntimeError(f"任务失败: {result.get('error')}")
        else:
            print(f"  … {task_id[:16]} status={st}")
    raise TimeoutError(f"任务 {task_id} 超时")

def upload_to_storage(image_url: str, file_path: str) -> str:
    """下载图片并上传到 Supabase Storage，返回公开 URL"""
    img_data = requests.get(image_url, timeout=60).content
    upload_url = f"{SUPABASE_URL}/storage/v1/object/{BUCKET}/{file_path}"
    headers = {
        "apikey":        SUPABASE_ANON_KEY,
        "Authorization": f"Bearer {SUPABASE_ANON_KEY}",
        "Content-Type":  "image/jpeg",
        "x-upsert":      "true",
    }
    r = requests.post(upload_url, headers=headers, data=img_data, timeout=60)
    if r.status_code not in (200, 201):
        raise RuntimeError(f"Storage 上传失败 {r.status_code}: {r.text}")
    public_url = f"{SUPABASE_URL}/storage/v1/object/public/{BUCKET}/{file_path}"
    return public_url

def ensure_bucket():
    """确保 storage bucket 存在"""
    url = f"{SUPABASE_URL}/storage/v1/bucket"
    headers = {
        "apikey":        SUPABASE_ANON_KEY,
        "Authorization": f"Bearer {SUPABASE_ANON_KEY}",
        "Content-Type":  "application/json",
    }
    body = {"id": BUCKET, "name": BUCKET, "public": True}
    r = requests.post(url, headers=headers, json=body, timeout=15)
    if r.status_code in (200, 201):
        print(f"✓ Bucket '{BUCKET}' 已创建")
    elif r.status_code == 409 or "already exists" in r.text.lower() or "Duplicate" in r.text:
        print(f"✓ Bucket '{BUCKET}' 已存在")
    else:
        print(f"⚠ Bucket 创建响应 {r.status_code}: {r.text}")

def db_delete_all():
    url = f"{SUPABASE_URL}/rest/v1/style_configs"
    params = {"id": "neq.impossible_placeholder"}
    headers = {**REST_HEADERS, "Prefer": "return=minimal"}
    r = requests.delete(url, headers=headers, params=params, timeout=15)
    print(f"  清空旧数据 → {r.status_code}")

def db_insert(rows: list):
    url = f"{SUPABASE_URL}/rest/v1/style_configs"
    r = requests.post(url, headers=REST_HEADERS, json=rows, timeout=15)
    print(f"  插入新数据 → {r.status_code}: {r.text[:120]}")

# ─── 主流程 ────────────────────────────────────────────
def main():
    print("=" * 60)
    print("🎨 开始批量生成风格预览图")
    print("=" * 60)

    # 1. 提交所有生成任务
    tasks = []
    for s in STYLES:
        print(f"  提交 [{s['label']}] …")
        try:
            tid = submit_task(s["prompt"])
            tasks.append({"style": s, "taskId": tid, "imageUrl": None, "storageUrl": None})
            print(f"    taskId = {tid[:20]}…")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"  ✗ 提交失败 [{s['label']}]: {e}")
            tasks.append({"style": s, "taskId": None, "imageUrl": None, "storageUrl": None})
        time.sleep(0.5)

    print(f"\n已提交 {sum(1 for t in tasks if t['taskId'])} / {len(tasks)} 个任务，等待生成…\n")

    # 2. 轮询结果
    for t in tasks:
        if not t["taskId"]:
            continue
        print(f"  轮询 [{t['style']['label']}] (taskId={t['taskId'][:16]}…)")
        try:
            t["imageUrl"] = wait_for_result(t["taskId"])
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"  ✗ 生成失败 [{t['style']['label']}]: {e}")

    # 3. 确保 bucket 存在
    print("\n检查 Storage Bucket …")
    ensure_bucket()

    # 4. 上传图片到 Storage
    print("\n上传图片至 Supabase Storage …")
    for t in tasks:
        if not t["imageUrl"]:
            continue
        file_path = f"styles/{t['style']['id']}.jpg"
        print(f"  上传 [{t['style']['label']}] → {file_path}")
        try:
            t["storageUrl"] = upload_to_storage(t["imageUrl"], file_path)
            print(f"    ✓ {t['storageUrl']}")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"  ✗ 上传失败 [{t['style']['label']}]: {e}")
            t["storageUrl"] = t["imageUrl"]  # fallback 使用原始 URL

    # 5. 全量替换数据库
    print("\n替换 style_configs 数据库 …")
    db_delete_all()

    rows = []
    for t in tasks:
        s = t["style"]
        preview = t.get("storageUrl") or t.get("imageUrl") or ""
        rows.append({
            "id":          s["id"],
            "label":       s["label"],
            "description": s["description"],
            "color":       s["color"],
            "tags":        s["tags"],
            "sort_order":  s["sort_order"],
            "is_active":   True,
            "preview_url": preview,
            "video_url":   None,
        })

    db_insert(rows)

    # 6. 汇总
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("✅ 完成！汇总结果：")
    for t in tasks:
        ok = "✓" if t.get("storageUrl") or t.get("imageUrl") else "✗"
        print(f"  {ok} [{t['style']['label']:8}] {(t.get('storageUrl') or '')[:70]}")
    print("=" * 60)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

```

```
    "X-Gateway-Authorization": f"Bearer {INTEGRATIONS_API_KEY}",
}

STYLES = [
    {"id":"anime",       "label":"二次元",  "description":"日系动漫风格，色彩鲜明，线条细腻",     "color":"from-violet-500 to-purple-600","tags":["日系动漫","细腻人物","ACG风格"],     "sort_order":1,  "prompt":"a young girl with long flowing hair standing under cherry blossom tree, anime style, cel shading, vibrant colors, beautiful detailed face"},

def submit(prompt):
    r = requests.post(SUBMIT_URL, headers=GEN_HEADERS,
                      json={"contents":[{"parts":[{"text":prompt}]}]}, timeout=30)
    r.raise_for_status()
    d = r.json()
    assert d["status"] == 0, d
    return d["data"]["taskId"]

def wait_result(tid, timeout=600):
    deadline = time.time() + timeout
    while time.time() < deadline:
        time.sleep(8)
        r = requests.post(QUERY_URL, headers=GEN_HEADERS, json={"taskId": tid}, timeout=30)
        d = r.json()["data"]
        st = d["status"]
        if st == "SUCCESS":
            return d["result"]["imageUrl"]
        if st == "FAILED":
            raise RuntimeError(f"FAILED: {d.get('error')}")
        print(f"    {tid[:20]}… {st}")
    raise TimeoutError(tid)

def upload_storage(img_url, path):
    data = requests.get(img_url, timeout=60).content
    up_url = f"{SUPABASE_URL}/storage/v1/object/{BUCKET}/{path}"
    r = requests.post(up_url, headers={
        "apikey": SUPABASE_ANON_KEY,
        "Authorization": f"Bearer {SUPABASE_ANON_KEY}",
        "Content-Type": "image/jpeg",
        "x-upsert": "true",
    }, data=data, timeout=60)
    if r.status_code not in (200, 201):
        raise RuntimeError(f"{r.status_code}: {r.text}")
    return f"{SUPABASE_URL}/storage/v1/object/public/{BUCKET}/{path}"

result_map = {}  # id -> final_url

# 1. Submit all
print("── 提交任务 ──────────────────────────────")
task_map = {}
for s in STYLES:
    tid = submit(s["prompt"])
    task_map[s["id"]] = tid
    print(f"  {s['label']:8} {tid}")
    time.sleep(0.3)

# 2. Poll all
print("\n── 等待生成 ──────────────────────────────")
for s in STYLES:
    sid = s["id"]
    tid = task_map[sid]
    print(f"  {s['label']:8} 轮询中…")
    try:
        url = wait_result(tid)
        result_map[sid] = url
        print(f"  {s['label']:8} ✓ {url[:80]}")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"  {s['label']:8} ✗ {e}")
        result_map[sid] = ""

# 3. Upload to Storage
print("\n── 上传 Storage ──────────────────────────")
for s in STYLES:
    sid = s["id"]
    cdn_url = result_map.get(sid, "")
    if not cdn_url:
        print(f"  {s['label']:8} 跳过（无URL）")
        continue
    try:
        pub_url = upload_storage(cdn_url, f"styles/{sid}.jpg")
        result_map[sid] = pub_url
        print(f"  {s['label']:8} ✓ {pub_url}")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"  {s['label']:8} ⚠ Storage失败，保留CDN: {e}")
        # keep cdn url

# 4. Save JSON for DB insert via SQL
output = []
for s in STYLES:
    output.append({
        "id":          s["id"],
        "label":       s["label"],
        "description": s["description"],
        "color":       s["color"],
        "tags":        s["tags"],
        "sort_order":  s["sort_order"],
        "is_active":   True,
        "preview_url": result_map.get(s["id"], ""),
        "video_url":   None,
    })

with open("/workspace/app-brhf2ms7ez29/tasks/style_data.json", "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
    json.dump(output, f, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)
print("\n✅ 数据已保存至 tasks/style_data.json")
print(json.dumps(output, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2))
```

    supabase
      .from('style_configs')
      .select('id, label, description, color, preview_url, video_url, tags, sort_order')
      .eq('is_active', true)
      .order('sort_order')
      .then(({ data }) => {
        if (data && data.length > 0) {
          setDynamicStyles(data.map(s => ({
            id: s.id,
            label: s.label,
            desc: s.description,
            color: s.color,
            previewUrl: s.preview_url,
            videoUrl: s.video_url ?? undefined,
            tags: s.tags ?? [],
          })));
        }
      });
    return () => clearTimeout(timer);

import { Dialog, DialogContent } from '@/components/ui/dialog';
import { Badge } from '@/components/ui/badge';
import { X, ZoomIn, Play, Pause, Volume2, VolumeX, Maximize2, Film } from 'lucide-react';
import { useEffect, useRef, useState, useCallback } from 'react';

export interface StyleItem {
  id: string;
  label: string;
  desc: string;
  color: string;
  previewUrl: string;
  videoUrl?: string;   // 可选的动态效果演示视频
  tags?: string[];
}

interface StylePreviewDialogProps {
  style: StyleItem | null;
  onClose: () => void;
}

type PreviewTab = 'video' | 'image';

export default function StylePreviewDialog({ style, onClose }: StylePreviewDialogProps) {
  const [tab, setTab] = useState<PreviewTab>('video');
  const [playing, setPlaying] = useState(false);
  const [muted, setMuted] = useState(true);
  const [progress, setProgress] = useState(0);
  const [videoLoaded, setVideoLoaded] = useState(false);
  const [videoError, setVideoError] = useState(false);
  const videoRef = useRef<HTMLVideoElement>(null);

  // 切换风格时重置状态
  useEffect(() => {
    setProgress(0);
    setPlaying(false);
    setVideoLoaded(false);
    setVideoError(false);
    setTab(style?.videoUrl ? 'video' : 'image');
  }, [style?.id]);

  // Dialog 打开后自动播放
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!style || tab !== 'video' || !videoRef.current) return;
    const v = videoRef.current;
    v.currentTime = 0;
    const play = async () => {
      try { await v.play(); setPlaying(true); } catch { /* autoplay blocked */ }
    };
    if (videoLoaded) play();
  }, [tab, videoLoaded, style?.id]);

  const handleTimeUpdate = useCallback(() => {
    const v = videoRef.current;
    if (!v || !v.duration) return;
    setProgress((v.currentTime / v.duration) * 100);
  }, []);

  const togglePlay = useCallback(() => {
    const v = videoRef.current;
    if (!v) return;
    if (v.paused) { v.play(); setPlaying(true); }
    else           { v.pause(); setPlaying(false); }
  }, []);

  const handleSeek = useCallback((e: React.MouseEvent<HTMLDivElement>) => {
    const v = videoRef.current;
    if (!v || !v.duration) return;
    const rect = e.currentTarget.getBoundingClientRect();
    const ratio = (e.clientX - rect.left) / rect.width;
    v.currentTime = ratio * v.duration;
    setProgress(ratio * 100);
  }, []);

  const handleClose = () => {
    videoRef.current?.pause();
    onClose();
  };

  const hasVideo = !!style?.videoUrl && !videoError;

   280 interface StyleCardProps {
   281   style: StyleItem;
   282   selected: boolean;
   283   onSelect: () => void;

   286 
   287 export function StyleCard({ style, selected, onSelect, onPreview }: StyleCardProps) {
   288   // 追踪"刚刚选中/取消"以触发单次弹跳动画
   289   const [animState, setAnimState] = useState<'idle' | 'selecting' | 'deselecting'>('idle');
   290   const prevSelected = useRef(selected);
   291   // 徽章每次从 false→true 都重新 mount，key 自增保证动画重放
   292   const [badgeKey, setBadgeKey] = useState(0);
   293 
   294   useEffect(() => {
   295     if (prevSelected.current === selected) return;
   296     if (selected) {
   297       setAnimState('selecting');
   298       setBadgeKey(k => k + 1);
   299       const t = setTimeout(() => setAnimState('idle'), 420);
   300       prevSelected.current = true;
   301       return () => clearTimeout(t);
   302     } else {
   303       setAnimState('deselecting');
   304       const t = setTimeout(() => setAnimState('idle'), 320);
   305       prevSelected.current = false;
   306       return () => clearTimeout(t);
   307     }
   308   }, [selected]);
   309 
   310   const cardAnim =
   311     animState === 'selecting'   ? 'animate-card-select' :
   312     animState === 'deselecting' ? 'animate-card-deselect' : '';
   313 
   314   const hasVideo = !!style.videoUrl;
   315 
   316   return (
   317     <div
   318       className={[
   319         'relative rounded-2xl overflow-hidden cursor-pointer group',
   320         selected && animState === 'idle'
   321           ? 'animate-ring-breathe'
   322           : selected
   323             ? 'ring-2 ring-primary shadow-[0_0_16px_hsl(var(--primary)/0.3)]'
   324             : 'ring-1 ring-border/60 hover:ring-primary/40',
   325         !selected ? 'hover:shadow-card transition-shadow duration-300' : '',
   326         cardAnim,
   327         'will-change-transform',
   328       ].filter(Boolean).join(' ')}
   329       style={{ transformOrigin: 'center center' }}
   330       onClick={onSelect}
   331     >
   332       {/* 缩略图 */}
   333       <div className="aspect-video w-full overflow-hidden bg-muted">
   334         <img
   335           src={style.previewUrl}
   336           alt={style.label}
   337           className={[
   338             'w-full h-full object-cover',
   339             'transition-[transform,filter] duration-500 ease-out',
   340             'group-hover:scale-[1.07] group-hover:brightness-110 group-hover:saturate-110',
   341             selected ? 'scale-[1.03]' : '',
   342           ].filter(Boolean).join(' ')}
   343         />
   344       </div>
   345 
   346       {/* 选中时的渐变覆层 */}
   347       <div
   348         className={[
   349           'absolute inset-0 transition-opacity duration-300 pointer-events-none',
   350           'bg-gradient-to-br from-primary/10 via-transparent to-cyan-500/8',
   351           selected ? 'opacity-100' : 'opacity-0',
   352         ].join(' ')}
   353       />
   354 
   355       {/* 预览按钮：有视频→Play，无视频→ZoomIn */}
   356       <button
   357         type="button"
   358         onClick={e => { e.stopPropagation(); onPreview(); }}
   359         className="absolute top-2 right-2 w-7 h-7 rounded-full bg-black/50 backdrop-blur-sm flex items-center justify-center opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-[opacity,transform] duration-200 group-hover:scale-100 scale-75 hover:bg-black/75 ring-1 ring-white/15"
   360         aria-label={hasVideo ? `播放${style.label}视频演示` : `预览${style.label}大图`}
   361       >
   362         {hasVideo
   363           ? <Play className="w-3.5 h-3.5 text-white/90 fill-white/90 ml-0.5" />
   364           : <ZoomIn className="w-3.5 h-3.5 text-white/85" />
   365         }
   366       </button>
   367 
   368       {/* 有视频时左下角显示 VIDEO 角标 */}
   369       {hasVideo && (
   370         <div className="absolute bottom-10 left-2 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity duration-200">

   372             <Film className="w-2.5 h-2.5" /> 视频
   373           </Badge>
   374         </div>
   375       )}

    30   { id: 'oilpainting', label: '油画插画',   emoji: '🖼️', desc: '厚重笔触，艺术质感' },
    31   { id: 'cyberpunk',   label: '赛博朋克',   emoji: '🤖', desc: '霓虹未来，暗黑科技' },
    32   { id: 'chinese',     label: '国风水墨',   emoji: '🏮', desc: '传统笔墨，东方意境' },
    33   { id: '3d',          label: '3D 渲染',    emoji: '💎', desc: '立体逼真，体积光效' },
    34   { id: 'pixel',       label: '像素艺术',   emoji: '🕹️', desc: '复古游戏，像素风格' },
    35   { id: 'sketch',      label: '黑白素描',   emoji: '✏️', desc: '素描线稿，简洁单色' },
    36 ];
    37 
    38 const RATIOS = [
    39   { id: '1:1',  label: '1:1',  desc: '方形' },
    40   { id: '4:3',  label: '4:3',  desc: '横版' },
    41   { id: '3:4',  label: '3:4',  desc: '竖版' },
    42   { id: '16:9', label: '16:9', desc: '宽屏' },
    43   { id: '9:16', label: '9:16', desc: '手机' },
    44 ];
    45 
    46 const COUNTS = [1, 2, 4];
    47 
    48 const QUALITIES = [
    49   { id: 'standard',  label: '标准',   multiplier: 1.0 },
    50   { id: 'fine',      label: '精细',   multiplier: 1.5 },
    51   { id: 'superfine', label: '超精细', multiplier: 2.5 },
    52 ];
    53 
    54 const BASE_CREDITS_PER_IMAGE = 3;
    55 const MAX_BATCH = 10;
    56 
    57 function calcCredits(count: number, quality: string, channelBase?: number): number {
    58   const q = QUALITIES.find(q => q.id === quality) ?? QUALITIES[0];
    59   const base = channelBase ?? BASE_CREDITS_PER_IMAGE;
    60   return Math.ceil(base * count * q.multiplier);
    61 }
    62 
    63 // ─── 批量任务类型 ──────────────────────────────────────
    64 type BatchStatus = 'pending' | 'running' | 'done' | 'failed';
    65 
    66 interface BatchItem {
    67   id:        string;
    68   prompt:    string;
    69   status:    BatchStatus;
    70   imageUrls: string[];
    71   error:     string;
    72 }
    73 
    74 // ─── 批量任务状态图标 ──────────────────────────────────
    75 function BatchStatusIcon({ status }: { status: BatchStatus }) {
    76   if (status === 'pending')  return <Clock       className="w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground shrink-0" />;
    77   if (status === 'running')  return <Loader2     className="w-4 h-4 text-primary animate-spin shrink-0" />;
    78   if (status === 'done')     return <CheckCircle2 className="w-4 h-4 text-emerald-400 shrink-0" />;
    79   return <AlertTriangle className="w-4 h-4 text-destructive shrink-0" />;
    80 }

```
    supabase
      .from('style_configs')
      .select('id, label, description, color, preview_url, video_url, tags, sort_order')
      .eq('is_active', true)
      .order('sort_order')
      .then(({ data }) => {
        if (data && data.length > 0) {
          setDynamicStyles(data.map(s => ({
            id: s.id,
            label: s.label,
            desc: s.description,
            color: s.color,
            previewUrl: s.preview_url ?? '',
            videoUrl: s.video_url ?? undefined,
            tags: s.tags ?? [],
          })));
        }
        setStylesReady(true);
      });
    return () => clearTimeout(timer);
  }, []);
```

<IMAGE_UPLOAD_REQUIREMENTS>
* IMAGE REQUIREMENT DETECTION:
  - Treat the system as requiring image upload functionality when the user explicitly or implicitly mentions: "image", "picture", "photo", "avatar", "banner", "thumbnail", "upload image", "manage pictures".
  - If any table contains image fields or any feature requires uploading, editing, or managing images, an **image upload subsystem** must be included.

* IMAGE PLATFORM & ARCHITECTURE RULES:
  1. **Mandatory Supabase Storage**
     - All image uploads must use **Supabase Storage** buckets.
     - Buckets must be created using `supabase_apply_migration`.
  2. **Bucket Policies**
     - Images usually don't require access control.
     - For private scenarios, generate a signed URL when loading images.
  3. **File Size & Format**
     - By default, the maximum upload size must be enforced according to the bucket configuration (default: **1 MB**).
     - If users attempt to upload files exceeding the limit, an **automatic compression strategy must be triggered**:
       - Convert images to **WEBP** format.
       - Restrict maximum resolution to **1080p** (preserve aspect ratio).
       - Apply quality setting = **0.8** and auto-degrade iteratively until the file size is below 1 MB.
     - Supported formats for upload: JPEG, PNG, GIF, WEBP, AVIF.
     - Filename Rules: Ensure that the uploaded file's name contains only English letters and numbers.
* ADDITIONAL FRONTEND INTEGRATION RULES:
  - A clear **Upload Button** must be designed.
    - Display **upload progress bar** in real-time.
    - Notify users explicitly on **upload success** or **failure**.
    - If compression is applied:
      - Inform users that the image was compressed automatically.
      - Display the **final file size** after compression in the confirmation message.

* IMAGE IMPLEMENTATION WORKFLOW
### Step 1: Initialize Supabase
- Ensure Supabase is properly initialized and connected to the frontend.

### Step 2: Bucket & Database Setup
- Use `supabase_apply_migration` to create a dedicated image bucket.
- Modify relevant tables to store image URLs/paths.
- Apply appropriate policies for read/write access.

### Step 3: File Validation
- Validate file size, type, and dimensions before upload.
- If the file exceeds the maximum allowed size, trigger the **automatic compression strategy** to reduce size to under 1 MB.

### Step 4: Frontend Implementation
- Implement the upload button with progress bar.
- Show **upload success/failure notification**.
- If compression was applied, notify the user and show the **compressed file size**.

### Step 5: User Guidance
- Provide clear instructions to the user about supported file formats and maximum size.
- Inform users about the automatic compression mechanism.

Old String: ```
const BASE_CREDITS_PER_IMAGE = 3;

```
New String: ```
const BASE_CREDITS_PER_IMAGE = 3;
const MAX_BATCH = 10;

// 自定义风格 ID
const CUSTOM_STYLE_ID = '__custom__';
// 用户上传最大文件尺寸（10MB）
const MAX_FILE_SIZE = 10 * 1024 * 1024;
// Storage 单文件限制（1MB），超出时压缩
const STORAGE_LIMIT = 1 * 1024 * 1024;

/** 将 File 压缩到 ≤ STORAGE_LIMIT，返回 Blob（WebP）*/
async function compressImage(file: File, onProgress?: (p: number) => void): Promise<{ blob: Blob; compressed: boolean; finalSize: number }> {
  const img = await new Promise<HTMLImageElement>((res, rej) => {
    const i = new Image();
    i.onload  = () => res(i);
    i.onerror = rej;
    i.src = URL.createObjectURL(file);
  });

  const MAX_SIDE = 1080;
  let w = img.naturalWidth;
  let h = img.naturalHeight;
  if (w > MAX_SIDE || h > MAX_SIDE) {
    const r = Math.min(MAX_SIDE / w, MAX_SIDE / h);
    w = Math.round(w * r);
    h = Math.round(h * r);
  }

  const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
  canvas.width  = w;
  canvas.height = h;
  canvas.getContext('2d')!.drawImage(img, 0, 0, w, h);

  // 从 0.9 逐步降质直到 ≤ STORAGE_LIMIT
  let quality = 0.9;
  let blob: Blob | null = null;
  while (quality >= 0.4) {
    blob = await new Promise<Blob>(res =>
      canvas.toBlob(b => res(b!), 'image/webp', quality),
    );
    if (blob && blob.size <= STORAGE_LIMIT) break;
    quality -= 0.1;
    onProgress?.(Math.round((0.9 - quality) / 0.5 * 50));
  }

  URL.revokeObjectURL(img.src);
  return {
    blob:       blob ?? new Blob(),
    compressed: file.size > STORAGE_LIMIT,
    finalSize:  blob?.size ?? 0,
  };
}
```

```
      setUploadProgress(100);

        toast.success('参考图上传成功');
      }
    } catch (err) {
      toast.error(`上传失败：${String(err)}`);
    } finally {
      setUploadingRef(false);
      setUploadProgress(0);
      // 清空 input，允许同一文件再次触发
      if (fileInputRef.current) fileInputRef.current.value = '';
    }
  }, [user]);

  const handleFileChange = useCallback((e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {
    const file = e.target.files?.[0];
    if (file) handleCustomUpload(file);
  }, [handleCustomUpload]);

  const clearCustomRef = useCallback(() => {
    setCustomRefUrl(null);
    setStyle('anime');
    if (fileInputRef.current) fileInputRef.current.value = '';
  }, []);
```

New String: ```
  const stopPoll = useCallback(() => {
    if (pollIntervalRef.current) { clearInterval(pollIntervalRef.current); pollIntervalRef.current = null; }
  }, []);

  // ── 自定义参考图：上传处理 ────────────────────────────
  const handleCustomUpload = useCallback(async (file: File) => {
    if (!['image/jpeg', 'image/png', 'image/webp'].includes(file.type)) {
      toast.error('仅支持 JPG / PNG 格式');
      return;
    }
    if (file.size > MAX_FILE_SIZE) {
      toast.error('图片大小不能超过 10MB');
      return;
    }
    if (!user) { toast.error('请先登录'); return; }

    setUploadingRef(true);
    setUploadProgress(10);

    try {
      let uploadBlob: Blob = file;
      let compressed = false;
      let finalSize  = file.size;

      if (file.size > STORAGE_LIMIT) {
        toast.info('图片较大，正在自动压缩…');
        const result = await compressImage(file, p => setUploadProgress(10 + Math.round(p * 0.4)));
        uploadBlob  = result.blob;
        compressed  = result.compressed;
        finalSize   = result.finalSize;
        setUploadProgress(55);
      }

      const path = `${user.id}/style_ref_${Date.now()}.webp`;
      setUploadProgress(60);

      const { error: upErr } = await supabase.storage
        .from('user-style-refs')
        .upload(path, uploadBlob, { contentType: 'image/webp', upsert: true });

      if (upErr) throw new Error(upErr.message);
      setUploadProgress(95);

      const { data: urlData } = supabase.storage
        .from('user-style-refs')
        .getPublicUrl(path);

      setCustomRefUrl(urlData.publicUrl);
      setStyle(CUSTOM_STYLE_ID);
      setUploadProgress(100);

      toast.success(
        compressed
          ? `参考图已上传（已压缩至 ${(finalSize / 1024).toFixed(0)} KB）`
          : '参考图上传成功',
      );
    } catch (err) {
      toast.error(`上传失败：${String(err)}`);
    } finally {
      setUploadingRef(false);
      setUploadProgress(0);
      if (fileInputRef.current) fileInputRef.current.value = '';
    }
  }, [user]);

  const handleFileChange = useCallback(
    (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {
      const file = e.target.files?.[0];
      if (file) handleCustomUpload(file);
    },
    [handleCustomUpload],
  );

  const clearCustomRef = useCallback(() => {
    setCustomRefUrl(null);
    setStyle('anime');
    if (fileInputRef.current) fileInputRef.current.value = '';
  }, []);
```

    94 function TagInput({ tags, onChange }: { tags: string[]; onChange: (t: string[]) => void }) {
    95   const [input, setInput] = useState('');
    96 
    97   const add = () => {
    98     const v = input.trim();
    99     if (!v || tags.includes(v) || tags.length >= 6) return;
   100     onChange([...tags, v]);
   101     setInput('');
   102   };
   103 
   104   return (
   105     <div className="space-y-2">
   106       <div className="flex gap-2">
   107         <Input
   108           value={input}
   109           onChange={e => setInput(e.target.value)}
   110           onKeyDown={e => { if (e.key === 'Enter') { e.preventDefault(); add(); } }}
   111           placeholder="输入标签后按 Enter 添加（最多6个）"
   112           className="h-8 text-sm px-3"
   113           maxLength={12}
   114         />
   115         <Button type="button" variant="outline" size="sm" className="h-8 px-3 shrink-0" onClick={add}>
   116           <Plus className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
   117         </Button>
   118       </div>
   119       {tags.length > 0 && (
   120         <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1.5">
   121           {tags.map(tag => (
   122             <Badge
   123               key={tag}
   124               variant="secondary"
   125               className="text-xs bg-primary/10 text-primary border-primary/20 rounded-full pl-2.5 pr-1.5 gap-1"
   126             >
   127               {tag}
   128               <button
   129                 type="button"
   130                 onClick={() => onChange(tags.filter(t => t !== tag))}
   131                 className="w-3.5 h-3.5 rounded-full hover:bg-primary/20 flex items-center justify-center"
   132               >
   133                 <X className="w-2.5 h-2.5" />
   134               </button>
   135             </Badge>
   136           ))}
   137         </div>
   138       )}
   139     </div>
   140   );
   141 }

   143 // ─── 子组件：渐变色板选择器 ──────────────────────────
   144 function GradientPicker({ value, onChange }: { value: string; onChange: (v: string) => void }) {
   145   return (
   146     <div className="grid grid-cols-8 gap-1.5">
   147       {GRADIENT_PRESETS.map(g => (
   148         <button
   149           key={g.value}
   150           type="button"
   151           title={g.label}
   152           onClick={() => onChange(g.value)}
   153           className={[
   154             'w-full aspect-square rounded-md bg-gradient-to-br transition-transform duration-150',
   155             g.value,
   156             value === g.value
   157               ? 'ring-2 ring-offset-1 ring-offset-background ring-primary scale-110'
   158               : 'hover:scale-105',
   159           ].join(' ')}
   160         />
   161       ))}
   162     </div>
   163   );
   164 }
   165 
   166 // ─── 主组件 ───────────────────────────────────────────
   167 export default function AdminStylesPage() {
   168   const [styles, setStyles] = useState<StyleConfig[]>([]);
   169   const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
   170   const [uploadMap, setUploadMap] = useState<Record<string, UploadState>>({});
   171   const [previewStyle, setPreviewStyle] = useState<StyleItem | null>(null);
   172   const fileInputRefs = useRef<Record<string, HTMLInputElement | null>>({});
   173   const [dragOver, setDragOver] = useState<string | null>(null);
   174 
   175   // 新增画风 Dialog
   176   const [addOpen, setAddOpen] = useState(false);
   177   const [form, setForm] = useState<NewStyleForm>(EMPTY_FORM);
   178   const [tagInput] = useState('');
   179   const [saving, setSaving] = useState(false);
   180   const previewImgRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement | null>(null);
   181 
   182   // 删除确认
   183   const [deleteTarget, setDeleteTarget] = useState<StyleConfig | null>(null);
   184   const [deleting, setDeleting] = useState(false);
   185 
   186   // ── 加载 ──
   187   const loadStyles = useCallback(async () => {
   188     setLoading(true);
   189     const { data, error } = await supabase
   190       .from('style_configs')
   191       .select('*')
   192       .order('sort_order');
   193     if (error) toast.error('加载画风配置失败：' + error.message);
   194     else setStyles(data ?? []);
   195     setLoading(false);
   196   }, []);
   197 
   198   useEffect(() => { loadStyles(); }, [loadStyles]);
   199 
   200   // ── 工具：上传文件到 bucket ──
   201   const uploadFile = useCallback(async (
   202     path: string,
   203     file: File,
   204     onProgress: (p: number) => void,
   205   ): Promise<string | null> => {
   206     let fake = 0;
   207     const timer = setInterval(() => {
   208       fake = Math.min(fake + 12, 85);
   209       onProgress(fake);
   210     }, 180);
   211 
   212     const { error } = await supabase.storage
   213       .from(BUCKET)
   214       .upload(path, file, { cacheControl: '3600', upsert: false });
   215 
   216     clearInterval(timer);
   217     if (error) { onProgress(0); return null; }
   218 
   219     onProgress(100);
   220     const { data } = supabase.storage.from(BUCKET).getPublicUrl(path);
   221     return data.publicUrl;
   222   }, []);
   223 
   224   // ── 上传演示视频 ──
   225   const uploadVideo = useCallback(async (styleId: string, file: File) => {
   226     if (!file.type.startsWith('video/')) {
   227       toast.error('只支持视频文件（mp4 / webm / mov）'); return;
   228     }
   229     if (file.size > MAX_VIDEO_MB * 1024 * 1024) {
   230       toast.error(`视频不能超过 ${MAX_VIDEO_MB}MB`); return;
   231     }
   232 
   233     const ext = file.name.split('.').pop() ?? 'mp4';
   234     const path = `videos/${styleId}_${Date.now()}.${ext}`;
   235 
   236     setUploadMap(prev => ({ ...prev, [styleId]: { styleId, progress: 0, status: 'uploading' } }));
   237 
   238     // 删旧文件
   239     const existing = styles.find(s => s.id === styleId);
   240     if (existing?.video_url) {
   241       try {
   242         const old = new URL(existing.video_url).pathname.split(`/${BUCKET}/`)[1];
   243         if (old) await supabase.storage.from(BUCKET).remove([old]);
   244       } catch { /* ignore */ }
   245     }
   246 
   247     const url = await uploadFile(path, file, p =>
   248       setUploadMap(prev => ({ ...prev, [styleId]: { styleId, progress: p, status: 'uploading' } }))
   249     );
   250 
   251     if (!url) {
   252       setUploadMap(prev => ({ ...prev, [styleId]: { styleId, progress: 0, status: 'error', message: '上传失败' } }));
   253       toast.error('视频上传失败'); return;
   254     }
   255 
   256     const { error } = await supabase.from('style_configs')
   257       .update({ video_url: url, updated_at: new Date().toISOString() })
   258       .eq('id', styleId);
   259 
   260     if (error) {
   261       setUploadMap(prev => ({ ...prev, [styleId]: { styleId, progress: 0, status: 'error', message: error.message } }));
   262       toast.error('保存失败：' + error.message); return;
   263     }
   264 
   265     setUploadMap(prev => ({ ...prev, [styleId]: { styleId, progress: 100, status: 'success' } }));
   266     setStyles(prev => prev.map(s => s.id === styleId ? { ...s, video_url: url } : s));
   267     toast.success(`「${existing?.label}」演示视频上传成功`);
   268     setTimeout(() => setUploadMap(prev => { const n = { ...prev }; delete n[styleId]; return n; }), 3000);
   269   }, [styles, uploadFile]);
   270 
   271   // ── 删除演示视频 ──
   272   const removeVideo = useCallback(async (style: StyleConfig) => {
   273     if (!style.video_url) return;
   274     try {
   275       const old = new URL(style.video_url).pathname.split(`/${BUCKET}/`)[1];
   276       if (old) await supabase.storage.from(BUCKET).remove([old]);
   277     } catch { /* ignore */ }
   278     const { error } = await supabase.from('style_configs')
   279       .update({ video_url: null, updated_at: new Date().toISOString() })
   280       .eq('id', style.id);
   281     if (error) { toast.error('删除失败：' + error.message); return; }
   282     setStyles(prev => prev.map(s => s.id === style.id ? { ...s, video_url: null } : s));
   283     toast.success(`「${style.label}」演示视频已删除`);
   284   }, []);
   285 
   286   // ── 删除画风 ──
   287   const deleteStyle = useCallback(async () => {
   288     if (!deleteTarget) return;
   289     setDeleting(true);
   290     // 删除存储文件
   291     const paths: string[] = [];
   292     if (deleteTarget.preview_url) {
   293       try { paths.push(new URL(deleteTarget.preview_url).pathname.split(`/${BUCKET}/`)[1]); } catch { /* */ }
   294     }
   295     if (deleteTarget.video_url) {
   296       try { paths.push(new URL(deleteTarget.video_url).pathname.split(`/${BUCKET}/`)[1]); } catch { /* */ }
   297     }
   298     if (paths.filter(Boolean).length) {
   299       await supabase.storage.from(BUCKET).remove(paths.filter(Boolean));
   300     }
   301     const { error } = await supabase.from('style_configs').delete().eq('id', deleteTarget.id);
   302     setDeleting(false);
   303     if (error) { toast.error('删除失败：' + error.message); return; }
   304     setStyles(prev => prev.filter(s => s.id !== deleteTarget.id));
   305     toast.success(`画风「${deleteTarget.label}」已删除`);
   306     setDeleteTarget(null);
   307   }, [deleteTarget]);
   308 
   309   // ── 拖拽 ──
   310   const handleDrop = useCallback((e: React.DragEvent, styleId: string) => {
   311     e.preventDefault(); setDragOver(null);
   312     const file = e.dataTransfer.files?.[0] ?? null;
   313     if (file) uploadVideo(styleId, file);
   314   }, [uploadVideo]);
   315 
   316   // ── 新增画风 - 表单字段更新 ──
   317   const setField = <K extends keyof NewStyleForm>(key: K, val: NewStyleForm[K]) =>
   318     setForm(prev => ({ ...prev, [key]: val }));
   319 
   320   // 本地图片预览
   321   const handlePreviewImage = (file: File | null) => {
   322     if (!file) return;
   323     if (!file.type.startsWith('image/')) { toast.error('请上传图片文件'); return; }
   324     if (file.size > MAX_IMAGE_MB * 1024 * 1024) { toast.error(`图片不能超过 ${MAX_IMAGE_MB}MB`); return; }
   325     const url = URL.createObjectURL(file);
   326     setForm(prev => ({ ...prev, previewFile: file, previewPreview: url }));
   327   };
   328 
   329   // ── 新增画风 - 提交 ──
   330   const handleAddStyle = useCallback(async () => {
   331     // 校验
   332     if (!form.id.trim()) { toast.error('请填写画风 ID'); return; }
   333     if (!/^[a-z0-9-]+$/.test(form.id.trim())) { toast.error('ID 只能包含小写字母、数字和连字符'); return; }
   334     if (!form.label.trim()) { toast.error('请填写画风名称'); return; }
   335     if (!form.description.trim()) { toast.error('请填写描述'); return; }
   336     if (!form.previewFile) { toast.error('请上传预览图片'); return; }
   337 
   338     // 检查 ID 重复
   339     if (styles.some(s => s.id === form.id.trim())) {
   340       toast.error(`ID「${form.id}」已存在，请换一个`); return;
   341     }
   342 
   343     setSaving(true);
   344 
   345     // 上传预览图
   346     const imgExt = form.previewFile.name.split('.').pop() ?? 'jpg';
   347     const imgPath = `previews/${form.id.trim()}_${Date.now()}.${imgExt}`;
   348     const previewUrl = await uploadFile(imgPath, form.previewFile, () => {});
   349 
   350     if (!previewUrl) {
   351       toast.error('预览图上传失败'); setSaving(false); return;
   352     }
   353 
   354     // 确定排序号
   355     const maxOrder = styles.reduce((m, s) => Math.max(m, s.sort_order), 0);
   356     const sortOrder = form.sort_order > 0 ? form.sort_order : maxOrder + 1;
   357 
   358     // 写入 DB
   359     const { error } = await supabase.from('style_configs').insert({
   360       id: form.id.trim(),
   361       label: form.label.trim(),
   362       description: form.description.trim(),
   363       color: form.color,
   364       preview_url: previewUrl,
   365       video_url: null,
   366       tags: form.tags,
   367       sort_order: sortOrder,
   368       is_active: true,
   369     });
   370 
   371     setSaving(false);
   372 
   373     if (error) { toast.error('新增失败：' + error.message); return; }
   374 
   375     toast.success(`画风「${form.label}」新增成功`);
   376     setAddOpen(false);
   377     setForm(EMPTY_FORM);
   378     loadStyles();
   379   }, [form, styles, uploadFile, loadStyles]);
   380 
   381   // 关闭新增 Dialog 时清理 objectURL
   382   const handleCloseAdd = () => {
   383     if (form.previewPreview) URL.revokeObjectURL(form.previewPreview);
   384     setForm(EMPTY_FORM);
   385     setAddOpen(false);
   386   };
   387 
   388   // ── 预览转换 ──
   389   const toStyleItem = (s: StyleConfig): StyleItem => ({
   390     id: s.id, label: s.label, desc: s.description, color: s.color,
   391     previewUrl: s.preview_url, videoUrl: s.video_url ?? undefined, tags: s.tags,
   392   });
   393 
   394   const stats = {
   395     total: styles.length,
   396     withVideo: styles.filter(s => s.video_url).length,
   397   };
   398 
   399   // ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
   400   return (
   401     <div className="space-y-6">
   402       {/* 页头 */}
   403       <div className="flex flex-col md:flex-row md:items-center justify-between gap-3">
   404         <div>
   405           <h1 className="text-xl font-bold">画风配置</h1>
   406           <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground mt-0.5">
   407             管理创作页面的画风选项，上传演示视频或新增自定义画风
   408           </p>
   409         </div>
   410         <div className="flex items-center gap-2 self-start">
   411           <Button variant="outline" size="sm" onClick={loadStyles} className="gap-1.5">
   412             <RefreshCw className="w-3.5 h-3.5" /> 刷新
   413           </Button>
   414           <Button size="sm" onClick={() => setAddOpen(true)} className="gap-1.5">
   415             <Plus className="w-3.5 h-3.5" /> 新增画风
   416           </Button>
   417         </div>
   418       </div>
   419 
   420       {/* 统计条 */}
   421       <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-3">
   422         {[
   423           { label: '画风总数', value: stats.total, color: 'text-primary' },
   424           { label: '已上传视频', value: stats.withVideo, color: 'text-green-400' },
   425           { label: '待上传视频', value: stats.total - stats.withVideo, color: 'text-amber-400' },
   426         ].map(({ label, value, color }) => (
   427           <Card key={label} className="flex-1 min-w-[110px]">
   428             <CardContent className="p-4 text-center">
   429               <p className={`text-2xl font-bold ${color}`}>{value}</p>
   430               <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-0.5">{label}</p>
   431             </CardContent>
   432           </Card>
   433         ))}
   434       </div>
   435 
   436       {/* 说明 */}
   437       <div className="flex items-start gap-2 text-xs text-muted-foreground bg-muted/40 rounded-lg px-4 py-3 border border-border/50">
   438         <AlertCircle className="w-3.5 h-3.5 shrink-0 mt-0.5 text-primary/70" />
   439         <span>
   440           视频支持 MP4 / WebM / MOV，不超过 {MAX_VIDEO_MB}MB；
   441           预览图支持 JPG / PNG / WebP，不超过 {MAX_IMAGE_MB}MB。
   442           可将视频文件直接拖拽到卡片上快速上传。
   443         </span>
   444       </div>
   445 
   446       {/* 画风网格 */}
   447       {loading ? (
   448         <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-4">
   449           {Array.from({ length: 6 }).map((_, i) => (
   450             <Card key={i} className="animate-pulse">
   451               <CardContent className="p-4">
   452                 <div className="aspect-video bg-muted rounded-lg mb-3" />
   453                 <div className="h-4 bg-muted rounded w-1/3 mb-2" />
   454                 <div className="h-3 bg-muted rounded w-2/3" />
   455               </CardContent>
   456             </Card>
   457           ))}
   458         </div>
   459       ) : (
   460         <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-4">
   461           {styles.map(style => {
   462             const upload = uploadMap[style.id];
   463             const isDragTarget = dragOver === style.id;
   464             const hasVideo = !!style.video_url;
   465 
   466             return (
   467               <Card
   468                 key={style.id}
   469                 className={`overflow-hidden transition-colors duration-200 ${isDragTarget ? 'border-primary ring-2 ring-primary/30' : ''}`}
   470               >
   471                 <CardContent className="p-0">
   472                   {/* 预览区 */}
   473                   <div
   474                     className="relative aspect-video bg-muted overflow-hidden group/thumb"
   475                     onDragOver={e => { e.preventDefault(); setDragOver(style.id); }}
   476                     onDragLeave={() => setDragOver(null)}
   477                     onDrop={e => handleDrop(e, style.id)}
   478                   >
   479                     {style.preview_url ? (
   480                       <img src={style.preview_url} alt={style.label} className="w-full h-full object-cover" />
   481                     ) : (
   482                       <div className="w-full h-full flex items-center justify-center">
   483                         <ImageIcon className="w-8 h-8 text-muted-foreground/30" />
   484                       </div>
   485                     )}
   486 
   487                     {/* 拖拽遮罩 */}
   488                     {isDragTarget && (
   489                       <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-primary/20 backdrop-blur-sm flex flex-col items-center justify-center gap-2">
   490                         <Upload className="w-8 h-8 text-primary animate-bounce" />
   491                         <span className="text-sm font-medium text-primary">松开即可上传</span>
   492                       </div>
   493                     )}
   494 
   495                     {/* hover 操作层 */}
   496                     {!isDragTarget && (
   497                       <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-black/55 opacity-0 group-hover/thumb:opacity-100 transition-opacity duration-200 flex items-center justify-center gap-2">
   498                         <button onClick={() => setPreviewStyle(toStyleItem(style))}
   499                           className="w-9 h-9 rounded-full bg-white/15 hover:bg-white/25 backdrop-blur-sm flex items-center justify-center ring-1 ring-white/20 transition-colors" title="预览">
   500                           {hasVideo ? <Play className="w-4 h-4 text-white fill-white ml-0.5" /> : <Eye className="w-4 h-4 text-white" />}
   501                         </button>
   502                         <button onClick={() => fileInputRefs.current[style.id]?.click()}

                          </button>
                        )}
                      </div>

                        : <Badge className="text-[10px] h-5 px-2 bg-black/50 backdrop-blur-sm border-white/10 text-white/70 gap-1"><Film className="w-2.5 h-2.5" /> 待上传视频</Badge>

```
export default function AdminStylesPage() {
```

Thought: 现在在 `removeVideo` 函数后面添加 `uploadPreviewImage` 和 `removePreviewImage` 函数：

New String: ```
  // ── 删除演示视频 ──
  const removeVideo = useCallback(async (style: StyleConfig) => {
    if (!style.video_url) return;
    try {
      const old = new URL(style.video_url).pathname.split(`/${BUCKET}/`)[1];
      if (old) await supabase.storage.from(BUCKET).remove([old]);
    } catch { /* ignore */ }
    const { error } = await supabase.from('style_configs')
      .update({ video_url: null, updated_at: new Date().toISOString() })
      .eq('id', style.id);
    if (error) { toast.error('删除失败：' + error.message); return; }
    setStyles(prev => prev.map(s => s.id === style.id ? { ...s, video_url: null } : s));
    toast.success(`「${style.label}」演示视频已删除`);
  }, []);

  // ── 上传预览图 ──
  const uploadPreviewImage = useCallback(async (styleId: string, file: File) => {
    // 格式校验
    if (!['image/jpeg', 'image/png', 'image/webp'].includes(file.type)) {
      toast.error('上传失败：仅支持 JPG / PNG / WebP 格式');
      return;
    }
    // 大小校验（10MB）
    if (file.size > MAX_PREVIEW_MB * 1024 * 1024) {
      toast.error('图片大小超过限制，请重新选择（最大 10MB）');
      return;
    }

    const existing = styles.find(s => s.id === styleId);
    const ext  = file.name.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase() ?? 'jpg';
    const path = `previews/${styleId}_${Date.now()}.${ext}`;

    setImgUploadMap(prev => ({ ...prev, [styleId]: { styleId, progress: 0, status: 'uploading' } }));

    // 删除旧预览图（仅 style-assets bucket 内的文件）
    if (existing?.preview_url) {
      try {
        const oldPath = new URL(existing.preview_url).pathname.split(`/${BUCKET}/`)[1];
        if (oldPath) await supabase.storage.from(BUCKET).remove([oldPath]);
      } catch { /* 跨 bucket 的旧图忽略 */ }
    }

    const url = await uploadFile(path, file, p =>
      setImgUploadMap(prev => ({ ...prev, [styleId]: { styleId, progress: p, status: 'uploading' } })),
    );

    if (!url) {
      setImgUploadMap(prev => ({
        ...prev,
        [styleId]: { styleId, progress: 0, status: 'error', message: '上传失败，请重试' },
      }));
      toast.error('预览图上传失败');
      return;
    }

    const { error } = await supabase.from('style_configs')
      .update({ preview_url: url, updated_at: new Date().toISOString() })
      .eq('id', styleId);

    if (error) {
      setImgUploadMap(prev => ({
        ...prev,
        [styleId]: { styleId, progress: 0, status: 'error', message: error.message },
      }));
      toast.error('保存失败：' + error.message);
      return;
    }

    setImgUploadMap(prev => ({ ...prev, [styleId]: { styleId, progress: 100, status: 'success' } }));
    setStyles(prev => prev.map(s => s.id === styleId ? { ...s, preview_url: url } : s));
    toast.success(`「${existing?.label}」预览图上传成功！`);
    setTimeout(() => setImgUploadMap(prev => { const n = { ...prev }; delete n[styleId]; return n; }), 3000);
    // 清空 input 以允许同文件再次触发
    if (imgInputRefs.current[styleId]) imgInputRefs.current[styleId]!.value = '';
  }, [styles, uploadFile]);

  // ── 删除预览图 ──
  const removePreviewImage = useCallback(async (style: StyleConfig) => {
    if (!style.preview_url) return;
    try {
      const oldPath = new URL(style.preview_url).pathname.split(`/${BUCKET}/`)[1];
      if (oldPath) await supabase.storage.from(BUCKET).remove([oldPath]);
    } catch { /* 跨 bucket 或无效 URL 忽略 */ }
    const { error } = await supabase.from('style_configs')
      .update({ preview_url: '', updated_at: new Date().toISOString() })
      .eq('id', style.id);
    if (error) { toast.error('删除失败：' + error.message); return; }
    setStyles(prev => prev.map(s => s.id === style.id ? { ...s, preview_url: '' } : s));
    toast.success(`「${style.label}」预览图已删除`);
  }, []);
```
